=667  \\$aLetters written by author's great grandaughterto the ILL Dept.: "Hermann Morath [born Hirsh Morat in 1876] left Riga, Latvia for Denmark sometime in 1933 and died in Copenhagen on September 16, 1939 in the Copenhagen City Hospital and is buried in Mosaiske Vestre Cemetery in Copenhagen. All his grown children with spouses and his granchildren and his wife, Rachel, with the exception of my grandfather and his immediate family, perished in Riga Ghetto in 1941. My grandfather fled Riga 3 hours before Nazis came in and saved 3 of his daughters, one of which was my Mother. My grandfather died in Nahariya, Israel in 1982. My mother died in Philadelphia, U.S. In 1998. My only sister died in Philadelphia in 2008. When Hermann Morath died he made My mother a heir of whatever it was that he left in his Will. That's the basis of my claim to copyright . It is supported by my aunts, living in Israel, Aviva Vorkel of Rishon Le Zion and Esther Brant of Nahariya."
=667  \\$aLetter to Gifts Dept of NLI, dated March 18, 2014: Avi Sion is not only my nom de plume (the name I write under) but the name I am known by with all my acquaintances. Very few people know my first name Albert. I dislike the name Albert and have never identified with it. I am, to everyone, and even to myself, Avi. My name on my Swiss and Canadian passports is indeed Albert Sion, and I still therefore do use this name for official purposes (e.g. bank accounts, credit cards). But my name on my Israeli passport is Avraham Sion - whence the diminutive Avi. I officially changed my name from Albert to Avraham in Israel over thirty years ago. If you wish, I can send you a scan of my Israeli teudat zehut ID card. Avraham was, of course, unofficially, my Hebrew name from birth (after my grandfather) - and I use that for Torah purposes.
